  <script type="text/javascript">
    (function() {
        var contextPath = '/jira';
        var eventBuffer = [];

        function printDeprecatedMsg() {
            if (console && console.warn) {
                console.warn('DEPRECATED JS - contextPath global variable has been deprecated since 7.4.0. Use `wrm/context-path` module instead.');
            }
        }

        function sendEvent(analytics, postfix) {
            analytics.send({
                name: 'js.globals.contextPath.' + postfix
            });
        }

        function sendDeprecatedEvent(postfix) {
            try {
                var analytics = require('jira/analytics');
                if (eventBuffer.length) {
                    eventBuffer.forEach(function(value) {
                        sendEvent(analytics, value);
                    });
                    eventBuffer = [];
                }

                if (postfix) {
                    sendEvent(analytics, postfix);
                }
            } catch(ex) {
                eventBuffer.push(postfix);
                setTimeout(sendDeprecatedEvent, 1000);
            }
        }

        Object.defineProperty(window, 'contextPath', {
            get: function() {
                printDeprecatedMsg();
                sendDeprecatedEvent('get');
                return contextPath;
            },
            set: function(value) {
                printDeprecatedMsg();
                sendDeprecatedEvent('set');
                contextPath = value;
            }
        });
    })();

</script>

              <div id="descriptionmodule" class="module toggle-wrap">
               <div id="descriptionmodule_heading" class="mod-header">
                <ul class="ops"></ul>
                <h2 class="toggle-title">Description</h2>
               </div>
               <div class="mod-content">
                <div id="description-val" class="field-ignore-highlight"> 
                 <div class="user-content-block"> 
                  <p>This issue was original a scratch pad for various ideas for new Logos. It is now being used as a repository for submissions for the Solr Logo Contest...</p> 
                  <p> <a href="http://wiki.apache.org/solr/LogoContest" class="external-link" rel="nofollow">http://wiki.apache.org/solr/LogoContest</a></p> 
                  <p>Note that many of the images currently attached are not eligible for the contest since they do not meet the official guidelines for new Apache project logos (in particular that the full project name "Apache Solr" must be included in the Logo). Only eligible attachments will be included in the official voting.</p> 
                 </div> 
                </div> 
               </div>
              </div>

class=\\\"external-link\\\" rel=\\\"nofollow\\\"\u003ehttps:\\/\\/issues.apache.org\\/jira\\/secure\\/attachment\\/12349896\\/logo-solr-e.jpg\u003c\\/a\u003e and \u003ca rel=\\\"nofollow\\\"\u003ehttps:\\/\\/issues.apache.org\\/jira\\/secure\\/attachment\\/12358494\\/sslogo-solr.jpg\u003c\\/a\u003e, because they\'re simple and scale down well.  It should be possible to scale the logo, or a salient part of it, as small as a favicon (16x16) and still have it easily recognized.  Most of the designs above require a lot of pixels to be recognizable.  A good logo should be iconic more than textual--an abstract symbol.\u003c\\/p\u003e\\n\\n\u003cp\u003eOften you can sample an element of a logo to form a favicon (like we do with Lucene\'s \'L\').  So, when voting, think about whether there\'s an easily identifiable sample (e.g., is the typeface of the \'S\' distinctive?).\u003c\\/p\u003e\\n\\n\u003cp\u003eI note that Steve Stedman did not provide his logos under the Apache license. It should be possible to scale the logo, or a salient part of it, as small as a favicon (16x16) and still have it easily recognized.  Most of the designs above require a lot of pixels to be recognizable.  A good logo should be iconic more than textual--an abstract symbol. \\n\\n Often you can sample an element of a logo to form a favicon (like we do with Lucene\'s \'L\').  So, when voting, think about whether there\'s an easily identifiable sample (e.g., is the typeface of the \'S\' distinctive?). \\n\\n I note that Steve Stedman did not provide his logos under the Apache license.  Was that intentional?
